# Kim Kardashian

Kim Kardashian

American media personality (born 1980)

**Kimberly Noel Kardashian** (born October 21, 1980) is an American media personality, socialite, and businesswoman. She first gained media attention in 2007 following the unauthorized release of [a sex tape](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian,_Superstar "Kim Kardashian, Superstar") with American singer [Ray J](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ray_J "Ray J"). Afterwards, she and [her family](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kardashian_family "Kardashian family") began to appear on the [E!](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/E! "E!") reality television series _[Keeping Up with the Kardashians](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Keeping_Up_with_the_Kardashians "Keeping Up with the Kardashians")_. The show aired until 2021, and its success led to the formation of several [spin-offs](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spin-off_(media) "Spin-off (media)") before its revival in the form of, [Hulu](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hulu "Hulu")'s _[The Kardashians](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Kardashians "The Kardashians")_ (2022–present) as part of her and [her family](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kardashian-Jenner_family "Kardashian-Jenner family")'s multi-year deal with the streaming service.

Kardashian founded KKW Beauty and KKW Fragrance in 2017, both of which operated until 2022; the former was valued at over US$1 billion in 2021.[\[2\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-2)[\[3\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-3) She founded the shaping underwear and [foundation garment](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Foundation_garment "Foundation garment") company [Skims](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Skims "Skims") in 2019, which is valued at over US$4 billion as of 2023[\[update\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Kim_Kardashian&action=edit). Kardashian founded her skincare line, SKKN by Kim, in 2022.[\[4\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Johnson2022-4) She has released a variety of products tied to her name, including the 2014 [mobile game](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mobile_game "Mobile game") _[Kim Kardashian: Hollywood](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian:_Hollywood "Kim Kardashian: Hollywood")_, the 2015 photo book _[Selfish](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Selfish_(book) "Selfish (book)")_, and the 2015 emoji app [Kimoji](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kimoji "Kimoji"). Her acting credits include the films _[Disaster Movie](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disaster_Movie "Disaster Movie")_ (2008), _[Temptation: Confessions of a Marriage Counselor](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Temptation:_Confessions_of_a_Marriage_Counselor "Temptation: Confessions of a Marriage Counselor")_ (2013), [two _PAW Patrol_ films](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paw_Patrol#Films "Paw Patrol") (2021 and 2023), the [twelfth season](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Horror_Story:_Delicate "American Horror Story: Delicate") of the anthology horror series _[American Horror Story](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Horror_Story "American Horror Story")_ (2023–2024), and the legal drama series _[All's Fair](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/All's_Fair_(2025_TV_series) "All's Fair (2025 TV series)")_ (2025–present).

_[Time](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Time_(magazine) "Time (magazine)")_ magazine included Kardashian on their list of 2015's [100 most influential people](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Time_100 "Time 100").[\[5\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-5) She was named among _[Fortune](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fortune_(magazine) "Fortune (magazine)")_ magazine's Most Powerful Women in the world in 2023.[\[6\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-6) With a significant presence online and a large following across numerous social media platforms, she is the [eighth-most-followed individual on Instagram](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_most-followed_Instagram_accounts "List of most-followed Instagram accounts") and the [thirteenth-most-followed individual on Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_most-followed_Twitter_accounts "List of most-followed Twitter accounts").[\[7\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-guard-7)[\[8\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-et-8)[\[9\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-9) Both critics and admirers have described Kardashian as exemplifying the notion of being [famous for being famous](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Famous_for_being_famous "Famous for being famous").[\[10\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-10) She became a billionaire in 2021,[\[11\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-11) and is estimated by _[Forbes](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forbes "Forbes")_ to be worth US$1.7 billion as of May2025[\[update\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Kim_Kardashian&action=edit). Kardashian has become more politically active by lobbying for [prison reform](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prison_reform "Prison reform") and [clemency](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pardon "Pardon"),[\[12\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-12) and, in 2025, completed a four-year law apprenticeship that allows her to sit for the [California Bar Exam](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/State_Bar_of_California "State Bar of California"), which she did not pass.[\[13\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-NW-bar-fail-13)

## Early life and background

Kimberly Noel Kardashian was born on October 21, 1980, in Los Angeles, California, to [Robert](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Kardashian "Robert Kardashian") and [Kris Kardashian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kris_Kardashian "Kris Kardashian") (née Houghton).[\[14\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-14) She has an older sister, [Kourtney](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kourtney_Kardashian "Kourtney Kardashian"), a younger sister, [Khloé](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khlo%C3%A9_Kardashian "Khloé Kardashian"), and a younger brother, [Rob](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rob_Kardashian "Rob Kardashian").[\[15\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-15) Their mother is of [Scottish](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scottish_people "Scottish people") and [Dutch](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_people "Dutch people") ancestry,[\[16\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-16)[\[17\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-17) while their father is of [Armenian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenians "Armenians") descent.[\[18\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-18) In 1991, their parents divorced and their mother married [Caitlyn Jenner](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caitlyn_Jenner "Caitlyn Jenner"), the [1976 Summer Olympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1976_Summer_Olympics "1976 Summer Olympics") [decathlon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decathlon "Decathlon") winner then known as Bruce[\[a\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-20).[\[20\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-21) As a result of her mother's remarriage, Kim Kardashian acquired stepbrothers [Burt](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Burt_Jenner "Burt Jenner"), [Brandon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brandon_Jenner "Brandon Jenner"), and [Brody](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brody_Jenner "Brody Jenner"); stepsister Casey; and, later, two half-sisters, [Kendall](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kendall_Jenner "Kendall Jenner") and [Kylie Jenner](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kylie_Jenner "Kylie Jenner").[\[21\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-22)

Kardashian attended [Marymount High School](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marymount_High_School "Marymount High School"), a [Roman Catholic](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roman_Catholic "Roman Catholic") all-girls school in Los Angeles.[\[22\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-23) In 1994, her father represented football player [O. J. Simpson](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/O._J._Simpson "O. J. Simpson") during [his murder trial](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/O._J._Simpson_murder_case "O. J. Simpson murder case"). Simpson was Kardashian's godfather.[\[23\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-24) Kardashian's father died in 2003 of cancer.[\[24\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-25) In her teenage years, Kardashian was a close friend of [Nicole Richie](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nicole_Richie "Nicole Richie") and [Paris Hilton](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paris_Hilton "Paris Hilton"), through whom she first garnered media attention.[\[7\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-guard-7)[\[25\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-26) After she totaled her car at age 16, her father agreed to buy her a new one on the condition that she agree to be responsible for paying all expenses related to any future damages.[\[26\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-27) She subsequently began working at Body, a local clothing store in [Encino](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Encino,_Los_Angeles "Encino, Los Angeles"), an affluent Los Angeles neighborhood, where she worked for four years, assisting in the opening of the [Calabasas](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Calabasas,_California "Calabasas, California") location. In 2000, after entering into her first marriage, she resigned.[\[27\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-28)

## Career

### Beginnings (2003–2006)

By 2003, Kardashian was working as a [personal stylist](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Personal_stylist "Personal stylist") to the R&B singer and actress [Brandy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brandy_Norwood "Brandy Norwood"), the sister of [Ray J](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ray_J "Ray J").[\[28\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-29) Later, the siblings' mother (and manager) Sonja Norwood, alleged that in 2004 she had authorized Kardashian to make "one and only one" purchase on her [American Express](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Express "American Express") credit card and that nevertheless Kardashian and her sisters Khloé and Kourtney had incurred over $120,000 in [unauthorized charges](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Credit_card_fraud "Credit card fraud") to that card. Norwood also alleged that the bulk of the charges were attributable to purchases made at Kardashian's family-owned boutique in 2006 and 2007, after Kardashian was no longer employed by Norwood's daughter. Norwood further alleged that, at the request of her children, she did not file criminal charges, instead presenting her allegations personally to Kardashian, and that Kardashian apologized and promised to repay the debt. In 2008, when no payments had been made, Norwood filed a lawsuit. Kardashian has denied all these allegations. In 2009, the parties reportedly reached a confidential settlement and the lawsuit was dismissed.[\[29\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-30)[\[30\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-31)

In 2006, Kardashian began working as a stylist for [Paris Hilton](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paris_Hilton "Paris Hilton"), a childhood friend of hers. She appeared in several episodes of the reality series _[The Simple Life](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Simple_Life "The Simple Life")_ and was frequently photographed accompanying Hilton to events and parties.[\[31\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-32)[\[32\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-33) Sheeraz Hasan, a PR strategist working with Hilton, had previously met Kardashian and her mother Kris Jenner in 2005, and stated in a 2020 _[20/20](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/20/20_(American_TV_program) "20/20 (American TV program)")_ television special that Kardashian was "ready to do whatever it takes" to create a successful brand. Rick Mendozza, a freelance photographer on assignment for the tabloid [TMZ](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/TMZ "TMZ"), remarked in the same interview that, when Kardashian accompanied Hilton to nightclub Hyde, which was a [Hollywood](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hollywood,_Los_Angeles "Hollywood, Los Angeles") hotspot at the time, he continued to get assignments from tabloids to get photographs of Kardashian for the next three years.[\[33\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-34) In 2021, Kardashian said that Hilton "literally gave me a career. And I totally acknowledge that."[\[34\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-35)

### Breakthrough (2007–2010)

[![](https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/e9/Kim_Kardashian_6.jpg)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Kim_Kardashian_6.jpg) Kardashian at the Seventh Annual [Hollywood Life Magazine Awards](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hollywood_Life "Hollywood Life") in 2007

In February 2007, a [sex tape](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sex_tape "Sex tape") made by Kardashian and singer [Ray J](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ray_J "Ray J") in 2003 was [leaked](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet_leak "Internet leak") on the internet and gained national attention.[\[35\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-36)[\[36\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-37) Kardashian filed a lawsuit against [Vivid Entertainment](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vivid_Entertainment "Vivid Entertainment") for distributing the film as _[Kim Kardashian, Superstar](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian,_Superstar "Kim Kardashian, Superstar")_.[\[37\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-38) She dropped the suit 3 months later and [settled](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Settlement_(litigation) "Settlement (litigation)") for a reported US$5million, giving Vivid permission to market and sell copies of the tape.[\[38\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-upi-05-07-39) Sales from the film reportedly generated nearly US$1.5 million in revenue in the first six weeks.[\[39\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-40) Several media outlets later criticized her and her family for using the sex tape's release as a publicity stunt to promote their forthcoming reality show.[\[40\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-41)[\[41\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-42)[\[42\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-43)

In October 2007, Kardashian and her mother Kris Jenner, her step-parent Caitlyn Jenner (then Bruce Jenner), her siblings Kourtney, Khloé, and Rob Kardashian, and half-sisters Kendall and Kylie Jenner, began to appear in the reality television series _[Keeping Up with the Kardashians](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Keeping_Up_with_the_Kardashians "Keeping Up with the Kardashians")_.[\[43\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-44) The series proved successful for [E!](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/E! "E!"), and led to the creation of a number of spin-offs, including _Kourtney and Kim Take New York_ and _Kourtney and Kim Take Miami_.[\[44\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-45) The flagship series concluded in June 2021 after 294 episodes.[\[45\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-46)

Kardashian posed in a nude pictorial for the December 2007 issue of _[Playboy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Playboy "Playboy")_,[\[46\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-47)[\[47\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-48) and appeared on the cover of the November 2010 issue of Romanian _Playboy_, promoting a pictorial titled "Poezia Unui Fund Bombat" (The Poetry of a Bulging Ass).[\[48\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-49) She made her feature film debut, opposite [Carmen Electra](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carmen_Electra "Carmen Electra"), in the disaster film spoof _[Disaster Movie](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disaster_Movie "Disaster Movie")_ (2008), in which she appeared as a character named Lisa.[\[49\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-50)[\[50\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-51) In 2008, she was a participant on [season seven](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dancing_with_the_Stars_(American_season_7) "Dancing with the Stars (American season 7)") of _[Dancing with the Stars](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dancing_with_the_Stars "Dancing with the Stars")_, where she was partnered with [Mark Ballas](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mark_Ballas "Mark Ballas").[\[51\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-52) She was the third contestant to be eliminated.[\[52\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-usa30-53) In September 2009, Fusion Beauty and [Seven Bar Foundation](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seven_Bar_Foundation "Seven Bar Foundation") launched "Kiss Away Poverty", with Kardashian as the face of the campaign. For each LipFusion lipgloss sold, US$1 went to the Foundation to fund women entrepreneurs in the United States.[\[53\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-54) In October, she launched her first fragrance, self-titled "Kim Kardashian".[\[54\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Fragrances-55)[\[55\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-56) That year, she also released a workout DVD series, became a guest host–judge of [WrestleMania XXIV](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/WrestleMania_XXIV "WrestleMania XXIV") on _[America's Next Top Model](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/America's_Next_Top_Model "America's Next Top Model")_,[\[56\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Kim_Kardashian_Biography-57)[\[57\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-forbes-58)[\[58\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-59)[\[59\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-60) and guest-starred in _[How I Met Your Mother](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/How_I_Met_Your_Mother "How I Met Your Mother")_, _[Beyond the Break](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beyond_the_Break "Beyond the Break")_,[\[60\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Beyond-61) and [CBS](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CBS "CBS")'s _[CSI: NY](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CSI:_NY "CSI: NY")_.[\[61\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-megafon-62)[\[62\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-63)

[![](https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Kim_Kardashian_2010.jpg/500px-Kim_Kardashian_2010.jpg)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Kim_Kardashian_2010.jpg) Kardashian at an event for [The Heart Truth](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Heart_Truth "The Heart Truth") in 2010

By 2010, Kardashian had ventured into several new endorsement deals, including endorsing various food products for [Carl's Jr.](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carl's_Jr. "Carl's Jr.")[\[63\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-kimkardashianproducts-64)[\[64\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-65) On July 1, 2010, the New York City branch of [Madame Tussauds](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madame_Tussauds "Madame Tussauds") revealed a wax figure of Kardashian.[\[65\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-66) Kim, Kourtney, and Khloé wrote an autobiography titled _Kardashian Konfidential_, which was released in stores on November 23, 2010, and appeared on _[New York Times](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_York_Times "New York Times")_'s [Best Seller List](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_York_Times_Best_Seller_List "New York Times Best Seller List").[\[66\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-67) In December 2010, she filmed a music video for a song titled " [Jam (Turn It Up)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jam_(Turn_It_Up) "Jam (Turn It Up)")". The video was directed by [Hype Williams](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hype_Williams "Hype Williams"); [Kanye West](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kanye_West "Kanye West") makes a cameo in the video.[\[67\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-68) Kardashian premiered the song during a New Year's Eve party at TAO Las Vegas on December 31, 2010.[\[68\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-69) The song was produced by [The-Dream](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The-Dream "The-Dream") and [Tricky Stewart](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christopher_Stewart_(music_producer) "Christopher Stewart (music producer)"). When asked if an album was in the works, Kardashian replied, "There's no album in the works or anything—just one song we did for _Kourtney and Kim Take New York_, and a video Hype Williams directed, half of the proceeds we're giving away to a cancer foundation, because The-Dream's and one of my parents passed away from cancer. It's just all having fun—with a good cause".[\[69\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-70) Jim Farber, writing for the _[Daily News](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daily_News_(New_York) "Daily News (New York)")_, called the song a "dead-brained piece of generic dance music, without a single distinguishing feature", and suggested that the single made Kardashian the "worst singer in the reality TV universe".[\[70\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-71)

In 2010, Kardashian also served as producer for _[The Spin Crowd](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Spin_Crowd "The Spin Crowd")_, a reality television show about a New York City [public relations](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Public_relations "Public relations") firm run by [Jonathan Cheban](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jonathan_Cheban "Jonathan Cheban") and [Simon Huck](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_Huck "Simon Huck"), appeared on [season ten](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Apprentice_(U.S._season_10)#Episode_9:_Fragrant_Disregard "The Apprentice (U.S. season 10)") of _[The Apprentice](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Apprentice_(U.S._TV_series) "The Apprentice (U.S. TV series)")_,[\[71\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-72)[\[72\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-73) and guest starred with Khloé and Kourtney as themselves on the season three premiere episode of the series [_90210_](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/90210_(season_3) "90210 (season 3)").[\[73\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-74)

### Continued exposure (2011–2016)

In 2011, Kardashian released her third fragrance, "Gold",[\[54\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Fragrances-55) as well as a novel, [_Dollhouse_](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dollhouse_(book) "Dollhouse (book)"), along with sisters Kourtney and Khloé.[\[74\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-75) In 2012, _E!_ renewed _Keeping Up with the Kardashians_ for two additional seasons, in a deal reported to be worth $50 million.[\[75\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-76)[\[76\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-77) That year, Kardashian released her fourth fragrance, "True Reflection", which she worked with the company Dress for Success to promote,[\[77\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-78) and her fifth fragrance, "Glam", which was made available through [Debenhams](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Debenhams "Debenhams").[\[78\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-79) In _[Temptation: Confessions of a Marriage Counselor](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Temptation:_Confessions_of_a_Marriage_Counselor "Temptation: Confessions of a Marriage Counselor")_ (2013), a romantic drama produced, written, and directed by [Tyler Perry](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tyler_Perry "Tyler Perry"), Kardashian obtained the role of the co-worker of an ambitious therapist. While the film was a moderate box office success, with a worldwide gross of US$53.1 million,[\[79\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-80) critical response was negative and Kardashian won the [Razzie Award for Worst Supporting Actress](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Razzie_Award_for_Worst_Supporting_Actress "Razzie Award for Worst Supporting Actress").[\[80\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-81)

[![](https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Kim_Kardashian_West%2C_Parramatta_Westfield_Sydney_Australia_-_15035243919_%28cropped%29.jpg/500px-Kim_Kardashian_West%2C_Parramatta_Westfield_Sydney_Australia_-_15035243919_%28cropped%29.jpg)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Kim_Kardashian_West,_Parramatta_Westfield_Sydney_Australia_-_15035243919_(cropped).jpg) Kardashian in [Sydney](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sydney "Sydney"), [Australia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia "Australia"), in September 2014

Kardashian released _[Kim Kardashian: Hollywood](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian:_Hollywood "Kim Kardashian: Hollywood")_, a [mobile game](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mobile_game "Mobile game") for [iPhone](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IPhone "IPhone") and [Android](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Android_(operating_system) "Android (operating system)"), in June 2014. The objective of the game is to become a Hollywood star or starlet.[\[81\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Rothman-82) The game supports a [free-to-play](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_to_play "Free to play") model, meaning the game is free to download, but charges for in-game items.[\[82\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Mobilegamehit-83) It was a hit, earning US$1.6million in its first five days of release.[\[82\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Mobilegamehit-83) In July, developer [Glu Mobile](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Glu_Mobile "Glu Mobile") announced that the game was the fifth highest earning game in Apple's App Store.[\[82\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Mobilegamehit-83) She voiced an alien in the September 21, 2014, episode of the [adult animated](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adult_animation "Adult animation") series _[American Dad!](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Dad! "American Dad!")_.[\[83\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-variety1-84)[\[84\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-insidetv1-85)

Kardashian appeared on the cover and in a pictorial in _[Paper](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paper_(magazine) "Paper (magazine)")_'s winter 2014 issue, photographed by [Jean-Paul Goude](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jean-Paul_Goude "Jean-Paul Goude").[\[85\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-86) On the cover, her nude [buttocks](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Buttocks "Buttocks") are featured above the caption: " [Break the Internet](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Break_the_Internet "Break the Internet")", which generated considerable comment in both social and traditional media.[\[86\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-87)[\[87\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-papermag-88) A _Time_ magazine writer commented that, unlike previous celebrities' nudes that represented the women's rebellion against repressed society and "trying to tear down" barriers, Kardashian's exhibition was "just provocation and bluster, repeated images that seem to offer us some sort of truth or insight but are really just self serving. We want there to be something more, some reason or context, some great explanation that tells us what it is like to live in this very day and age, but there is not. Kim Kardashian's ass is nothing but an empty promise."[\[88\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-89) However, the stunt "set a new benchmark" in social media response,[\[89\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-90) and _Paper_'s website received 15.9 million views in one day, compared with 25,000 views on an average day.[\[90\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-91)[\[91\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-92)

Kardashian released a portfolio book called _Selfish_, a 325-page collection of self-taken photos of herself, in May 2015.[\[92\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-93) It received positive reviews from critics,[\[93\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-review_roundup-94) with Kat Brown of _[The Telegraph](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph "The Daily Telegraph")_ describing it as "unexpectedly revealing" and "oddly moving".[\[94\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-95) That year, she was also the cover model for the August issue of _[Vogue Spain](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Vogue_Espa%C3%B1a_(Spain)_cover_models "List of Vogue España (Spain) cover models")_,[\[95\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-96) and released an [emoji](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emoji "Emoji") pack for iOS devices called [Kimoji](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kimoji "Kimoji").[\[96\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Kimojii-97) The app was a best-seller, becoming one of the top 5 most bought apps in its first week of release.[\[96\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Kimojii-97)

By November 2016, as per [CBC Marketplace](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CBC_Marketplace "CBC Marketplace") and interviews with celebrity endorsement experts, Kardashian was reportedly paid at least US$300,000 for each post that she made on [Instagram](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Instagram "Instagram"), [Facebook](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Facebook "Facebook") and [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "Twitter"), endorsing beauty products like waist trainers, teeth whiteners as well as Coca-Cola and well-known charities.[\[97\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-CBC_News-98) [Business Insider](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Business_Insider "Business Insider") later estimated her fee to be around US$720,000 per [Instagram](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Instagram "Instagram") post. Even though engagement data indicates that her posts are worth slightly less,[\[98\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-99) her regular features in the news allow her to demand a premium above any calculated Instagram [sponsored post](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sponsored_post "Sponsored post") price.

### KKW Beauty, KKW Fragrances, and Skims (2017–2019)

With sisters [Kourtney](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kourtney_Kardashian "Kourtney Kardashian") and [Khloé](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khlo%C3%A9_Kardashian "Khloé Kardashian"), she launched the fashion boutique chain [Dash](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dash_(boutique) "Dash (boutique)") with an initial store in Calabasas, California.[\[56\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Kim_Kardashian_Biography-57) The chain operated between 2006 and 2018.[\[99\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-100) In 2017, Kardashian launched both her beauty and fragrance lines, KKW Beauty and KKW Fragrance.[\[100\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-101)[\[101\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-102)

Kardashian and [Laverne Cox](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Laverne_Cox "Laverne Cox") co-executive produced the [Lifetime](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lifetime_(TV_network) "Lifetime (TV network)") reality competition series, _Glam Masters_, which premiered in February 2018.[\[102\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-103) The eight-episode series revolved around aspiring beauty bloggers who competed for the title of "Glam Master"; prizes for the winner included collaborating with Kardashian on a makeup line for KKW Beauty and the opportunity to join her "glam squad".[\[103\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-104)[\[104\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-105) Kardashian and the series' winner, Argenis Pinal teamed up on an [eyeshadow sticks](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eye_shadow "Eye shadow") line for KKW Beauty, named "Créme Color Sticks".[\[105\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-106) She made a cameo appearance in the heist film _[Ocean's 8](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ocean's_8 "Ocean's 8")_, which was released on June 8, 2018.[\[106\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Petit2-107) Kardashian's next project was the [hidden camera](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hidden_camera "Hidden camera")- [prank](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Practical_joke "Practical joke") reality series, _[You Kiddin' Me](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/You_Kiddin'_Me "You Kiddin' Me")_. Co-executive produced by Kardashian and [Lionsgate Television](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lionsgate_Television "Lionsgate Television"), the web series premiered on [Facebook Watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Facebook_Watch "Facebook Watch") in September 2018.[\[107\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-108) She appeared alongside her sisters and mother Kris Jenner in the premiere episode of the series.[\[108\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-109) In November, Kardashian and Kris appeared in the [NBC](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NBC "NBC") special, _[A Legendary Christmas with John and Chrissy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Legendary_Christmas_with_John_and_Chrissy "A Legendary Christmas with John and Chrissy")_.[\[109\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-110)

In May 2019, Kardashian appeared in the music video for DJ duo [Dimitri Vegas & Like Mike](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dimitri_Vegas_&_Like_Mike "Dimitri Vegas & Like Mike") and [Paris Hilton](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paris_Hilton "Paris Hilton")'s single, " [B.F.A. (Best Friend's Ass)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/B.F.A._(Best_Friend's_Ass) "B.F.A. (Best Friend's Ass)")".[\[110\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-111) After announcing a new range of shapewear called Kimono in June, Kardashian was heavily criticized over the name of the brand, which critics argued disrespected Japanese culture and ignored the significance behind the [traditional outfit](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kimono "Kimono"). Following the launch of the range, the hashtag #KimOhNo began trending on [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "Twitter") and the mayor of [Kyoto](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kyoto "Kyoto") wrote to Kardashian to ask her to reconsider the trademark on Kimono. In response to public pressure, she announced that she would change the name.[\[111\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-112) However, Japanese trade minister [Hiroshige Seko](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hiroshige_Sek%C5%8D "Hiroshige Sekō") stated that he would still be dispatching patent officials for a meeting at the [U.S. Patent and Trademark Office](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Patent_and_Trademark_Office "United States Patent and Trademark Office"), and that Japan would keep an eye on the situation.[\[112\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-113) In August 2019, she rebranded the shapewear company to the name "Skims".[\[113\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-114)[\[114\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-115) Co-founded by Kardashian, British businesswoman [Emma Grede](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emma_Grede "Emma Grede"), and Swedish entrepreneur Jens Grede,[\[115\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-116) [Skims](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Skims "Skims") launched the following month as a [DTC](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Direct-to-consumer "Direct-to-consumer") operation via its webstore[\[116\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-117) and shortly after, was made available via multiple retail websites.[\[117\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-118) The brand has been recognized and praised for its inclusive sizing and apparel shades;[\[118\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-102020_voguebiz-119) its [celebrity branding](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celebrity_branding "Celebrity branding")—including musicians, actors, and athletes—has received significant media attention and achieved prominence in [popular culture](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Popular_culture "Popular culture").[\[119\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-120) Since its launch, Skims has expanded to a variety of loungewear, swimwear, activewear, women's apparel, menswear, and [unisex clothing](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unisex_clothing "Unisex clothing").[\[118\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-102020_voguebiz-119)[\[120\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-121)[\[121\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-122)

In February 2020, the brand entered its first retail partnership with luxury store chain [Nordstrom](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nordstrom "Nordstrom").[\[122\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-123)[\[123\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-124) Starting in 2021, it has opened various [pop-up stores](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pop-up_retail "Pop-up retail") in the United States, Europe and Asia.[\[124\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-125) Beginning in 2024, Skims has opened several retail stores across the US and the UK, with 22 outlets in the former.[\[125\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-126)[\[126\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-127) Under a deal, it provided Team USA-branded athleisure to the [US Olympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_at_the_Olympics "United States at the Olympics") team's female athletes at the [2020 Summer Olympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2020_Summer_Olympics "2020 Summer Olympics") and [Paralympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2020_Summer_Paralympics "2020 Summer Paralympics").[\[127\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-128) This partnership continued with multiple iterations of the [Winter Olympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winter_Olympic_Games "Winter Olympic Games"), the [Summer Olympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Summer_Olympic_Games "Summer Olympic Games"), and the [Paralympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paralympic_Games "Paralympic Games") throughout the 2020s decade. [2022 Winter Olympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2022_Winter_Olympics "2022 Winter Olympics"),[\[128\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-129) the [2024 Summer Olympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2024_Summer_Olympics "2024 Summer Olympics") and [Paralympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2024_Summer_Paralympics "2024 Summer Paralympics"),[\[129\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-130) and the [2026 Winter Olympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2026_Winter_Olympics "2026 Winter Olympics")[\[130\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-131) and four capsule collections released in collaboration with the [US Winter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_at_the_Winter_Olympics "United States at the Winter Olympics") and [Summer Olympics delegations](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_at_the_Summer_Olympics "United States at the Summer Olympics").[\[131\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-132)[\[132\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-133)[\[133\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-134) Skims has released collaborations with various brands and fashion houses including [Fendi](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fendi "Fendi"), [Dolce & Gabbana](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dolce_&_Gabbana "Dolce & Gabbana"), [Roberto Cavalli](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roberto_Cavalli_(company) "Roberto Cavalli (company)"), [Swarovski](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swarovski "Swarovski"), and [The North Face](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_North_Face "The North Face").[\[134\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-135)[\[135\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-136) In 2023, it entered a multiyear partnership as the official underwear partner of the [NBA](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Basketball_Association "National Basketball Association"), [WNBA](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Women's_National_Basketball_Association "Women's National Basketball Association"), and [USA Basketball](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USA_Basketball "USA Basketball").[\[136\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-137) In 2025, the company and [Nike](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nike,_Inc. "Nike, Inc.") introduced an activewear brand named NikeSkims—a joint operation.[\[137\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-138) For her work on Skims, Kardashian received the Brand Innovator award at the 2021 _[WSJ.](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/WSJ. "WSJ.")_ Innovator Awards and the Innovation Award at the 2023 [CFDA Awards](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CFDA_Awards "CFDA Awards").[\[138\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-139)[\[139\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-140) The company appeared in _[Time](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Time_(magazine) "Time (magazine)")_'s list of 100 Most Influential Companies of 2022,[\[140\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-141) and as of November 2025[\[update\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Kim_Kardashian&action=edit), is valued at US$5 billion.[\[141\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-142) As of 2024, Skims has generated "around $1 billion" in net sales.[\[142\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-143)

### _The Kardashians_ and acting ventures (2020–present)

On April 5, 2020, the documentary _Kim Kardashian West: The Justice Project_ premiered on [Oxygen](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oxygen_(TV_channel) "Oxygen (TV channel)"), starring and executive produced by Kardashian. It follows her journey advocating for [criminal justice reform](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Criminal_justice_reform "Criminal justice reform") and highlights [mass incarceration](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mass_incarceration "Mass incarceration") in the US.[\[143\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-144)[\[144\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-145) In September, she made a cameo appearance in the [YouTube Originals](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/YouTube_Originals "YouTube Originals") documentary, _[This is Paris](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/This_Is_Paris "This Is Paris")_.[\[145\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-146) In December 2020, it was announced that Kim, the Kardashian–Jenner sisters, and their mother Kris Jenner had signed a multi-year exclusive global content deal with Disney-owned [Hulu](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hulu "Hulu").[\[146\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-147) A reality television series titled _[The Kardashians](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Kardashians "The Kardashians")_ premiered in April 2022, co-produced by the sisters and Kris with British production company [Fulwell 73](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fulwell_73 "Fulwell 73").[\[147\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-148)[\[148\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-149) Described as a "premium version" of _Keeping Up with the Kardashians_,[\[149\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-150) the program had the most-watched series premiere for Hulu in its first three days in the US, and was the most-watched [Star Originals](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Star_(Disney+)_original_programming "List of Star (Disney+) original programming") series on Disney+ and Star+ across global markets.[\[150\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-151)As of November 2023[\[update\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Kim_Kardashian&action=edit), it is the most watched unscripted series in Hulu history.[\[151\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-152)

Kardashian appeared in the [Van Jones](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Van_Jones "Van Jones")–led documentary, _[The First Step](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_First_Step_(film) "The First Step (film)")_, which focuses on criminal justice reform; it premiered at the [Tribeca Film Festival](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tribeca_Festival "Tribeca Festival") in June 2021.[\[152\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-153) In July and August, she appeared in the premiere episodes of [Martha Stewart](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martha_Stewart "Martha Stewart")'s reality series, _[Martha Gets Down and Dirty](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martha_Gets_Down_and_Dirty "Martha Gets Down and Dirty")_; and Paris Hilton's cooking show _[Cooking with Paris](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cooking_with_Paris "Cooking with Paris")_, on [Discovery+](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discovery+ "Discovery+") and [Netflix](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netflix "Netflix").[\[153\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-154)[\[154\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-155)[\[155\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-156) Kardashian voiced Delores, a [poodle](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poodle "Poodle"), in the Canadian animated film _[PAW Patrol: The Movie](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PAW_Patrol:_The_Movie "PAW Patrol: The Movie")_, released on August 20, 2021.[\[156\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-157) Courtney Howard of _[Variety](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Variety_(magazine) "Variety (magazine)")_ stated that Kardashian and the supporting cast handled the film's "sillier moments".[\[157\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-158) She reprised her voice role in the film's sequel, _[PAW Patrol: The Mighty Movie](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PAW_Patrol:_The_Mighty_Movie "PAW Patrol: The Mighty Movie")_, released on September 29, 2023.[\[158\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-159) In October 2021, Kardashian hosted _Saturday Night Live_ and in her monologue, she made fun of her estranged-husband [Kanye West](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kanye_West "Kanye West"), her mother's ex-husband [Caitlyn Jenner](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caitlyn_Jenner "Caitlyn Jenner"), her sisters, [O. J. Simpson](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/O._J._Simpson "O. J. Simpson"), and many others.[\[159\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-160)

In January 2022, in a class-action lawsuit filed against the [cryptocurrency](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cryptocurrency "Cryptocurrency") company EthereumMax that alleged the company is a [pump and dump](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pump_and_dump "Pump and dump") scheme, Kardashian was named as a defendant, along with former professional boxer [Floyd Mayweather Jr.](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Floyd_Mayweather_Jr. "Floyd Mayweather Jr."), former [NBA](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Basketball_Association "National Basketball Association") player [Paul Pierce](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paul_Pierce "Paul Pierce"), and other celebrities, for [promoting](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/False_advertising "False advertising") the EthereumMax token on their various [social media accounts](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Influencer_marketing "Influencer marketing").[\[160\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-161) In October 2022, the [U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/U.S._Securities_and_Exchange_Commission "U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission") announced that Kardashian had agreed to pay a $1.26 million fine, to not promote cryptocurrency assets for three years, and to cooperate with an ongoing investigation without admitting or denying wrongdoing for failing to report receiving a $250,000 payment to promote the EthereumMax token.[\[161\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-162) In December 2022, [Central California U.S. District Court Judge](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_Central_District_of_California "United States District Court for the Central District of California") [Michael W. Fitzgerald](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_W._Fitzgerald "Michael W. Fitzgerald") dismissed the lawsuit on the basis that the claims were insufficiently supported given heightened [pleading standards](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pleading_(United_States) "Pleading (United States)") for fraud.[\[162\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-163)

In April 2022, Kardashian founded Skky Partners, a private equity firm, with a former partner of the [Carlyle Group](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Carlyle_Group "The Carlyle Group"). Her mother, Kris Jenner, is also a partner at the firm.[\[163\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-164) In December 2024, Kardashian stepped down as a managing partner and took on the role of senior operating advisor, whilst Jenner exited the firm.[\[164\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-165) In July 2022, she made her [Paris Fashion Week](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paris_Fashion_Week "Paris Fashion Week") modeling debut on the catwalk for fashion house [Balenciaga](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Balenciaga "Balenciaga").[\[165\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Paris_fashion_week_debut-166) The following month, Kardashian and [Beats Electronics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beats_Electronics "Beats Electronics") launched a collaborative range of [true wireless earbuds](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wireless_earbuds#True_wireless "Wireless earbuds") in an [earth tone](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Earth_tone "Earth tone") palette inspired by her "signature minimalist style".[\[166\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-167) In September, [Dolce & Gabbana](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dolce_&_Gabbana "Dolce & Gabbana") debuted its spring-summer 2023 collection, which Kardashian creative directed—taking after the fashion house's archive "with a retrospective of \[the years 1987–2007\]"—by leaning into an alter ego of "a sensual Italian mob wife".[\[167\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-168)[\[168\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-169) Under an exclusive deal with [Spotify](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spotify_Kids "Spotify Kids"), she hosted and co-produced the eight-episode podcast _The System: The Case of [Kevin Keith](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kevin_Keith "Kevin Keith")_ with network [Parcast](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parcast "Parcast").[\[169\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-170)[\[170\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-171) Premiering in October 2022, it outlines the discrepancies of Keith's case, in which he was convicted of triple homicide in 1994 in [Ohio](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ohio_River "Ohio River").[\[171\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-172)

Kardashian co-led the twelfth season of _[American Horror Story](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Horror_Story "American Horror Story")_, subtitled _[Delicate](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Horror_Story:_Delicate "American Horror Story: Delicate")_, alongside [Emma Roberts](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emma_Roberts "Emma Roberts").[\[172\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-173) Her first scripted television role, she played Siobhan Corbyn, the protagonist's best friend and publicist.[\[173\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-174) The season is based on Danielle Valentine's novel _Delicate Condition_; it was divided into two parts, which premiered in September 2023 and April 2024 on [FX](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FX_(TV_channel) "FX (TV channel)").[\[174\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-175)[\[175\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-176) Production for the season temporarily halted due to the [2023 Hollywood strikes](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2023_Hollywood_labor_disputes "2023 Hollywood labor disputes").[\[176\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-177) Kardashian's performance received positive reviews from critics.[\[177\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-178) Anthony D'Alessandro of _[Deadline Hollywood](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deadline_Hollywood "Deadline Hollywood")_ called her "perfect" for the role of Siobhan Corbyn;[\[178\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-179) whilst Coleman Spilde of _[The Daily Beast](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Daily_Beast "The Daily Beast")_ found Kardashian to be "the best part" of the season.[\[179\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-180) In August 2024, Kardashian signed a first-look TV deal with [20th Television](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/20th_Television "20th Television") to develop and produce scripted programming content.[\[180\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-181) The first project under this deal is the series _Group Chat_, based on [La La Anthony](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/La_La_Anthony "La La Anthony")'s 2014 book _The Love Playbook: Rules for Love, Sex and Happiness_. Intended for Hulu, Kardashian will executive produce the series alongside Kenya Barris and Anthony, the latter who will star in the project.[\[181\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-182) She again collaborated with Beats Electronics to release the "Beats x Kim" collection, a trio of [Beats Studio Pro](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beats_Electronics#Beats_Studio_Pro "Beats Electronics") headphones in nude tones.[\[182\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-183) On December 23, 2024, Kardashian released a cover version of " [Santa Baby](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Santa_Baby "Santa Baby")", produced by her brother-in-law [Travis Barker](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Travis_Barker "Travis Barker"), the husband of her sister [Kourtney](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kourtney "Kourtney").[\[183\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-184) Her first new music release since her 2011 debut single " [Jam (Turn It Up)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jam_(Turn_It_Up) "Jam (Turn It Up)")", its accompanying music video featured a cameo appearance by [Macaulay Culkin](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macaulay_Culkin "Macaulay Culkin").[\[184\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-santababy-185)

Kardashian co-executive produced and led the legal drama series, _[All's Fair](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/All's_Fair_(2025_TV_series) "All's Fair (2025 TV series)")_, created by [Ryan Murphy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ryan_Murphy_(producer) "Ryan Murphy (producer)"); it premiered on November 4, 2025, on Hulu in the US and Disney+ elsewhere.[\[185\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-186) She starred as Allura Grant, a divorce attorney and owner of an all-female law firm, alongside [Naomi Watts](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Naomi_Watts "Naomi Watts"), [Niecy Nash-Betts](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Niecy_Nash-Betts "Niecy Nash-Betts"), [Teyana Taylor](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Teyana_Taylor "Teyana Taylor"), [Sarah Paulson](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarah_Paulson "Sarah Paulson"), and [Glenn Close](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Glenn_Close "Glenn Close").[\[186\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-187) The series received overwhelmingly negative reviews from critics.[\[187\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-188) Angie Han of _[The Hollywood Reporter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Hollywood_Reporter "The Hollywood Reporter")_ wrote that the series was "brain dead" and described Kardashian's performance as "stiff and affectless without a single authentic note"[\[188\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-189) while Ed Power of _[The Telegraph](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph "The Daily Telegraph")_ called the program "a crime against television".[\[189\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-190) _All's Fair_ had the most-watched scripted Hulu series premiere of the past three years prior to its debut.[\[190\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-191) It was renewed for a second season.[\[191\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-192) In December 2025, Kardashian and [battle royale](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_royale_game "Battle royale game") game [Fortnite](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fortnite "Fortnite") launched her in-game bundle of cosmetics and outfits ("skins") as part of its Icon Series.

Kardashian will co-produce and star in the eponymous role—among a female ensemble cast—in the [Netflix](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netflix "Netflix") comedy film _The Fifth Wheel_, directed by [Eva Longoria](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eva_Longoria "Eva Longoria") and written by [Paula Pell](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paula_Pell "Paula Pell") and [Janine Brito](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Janine_Brito "Janine Brito").[\[192\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-193) She has committed to co-produce and star in an untitled [Amazon MGM Studios](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amazon_MGM_Studios "Amazon MGM Studios") thriller movie written by Natalie Krinsky "with \[her\] in mind".[\[193\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-194) Kardashian will also co-produce Amazon MGM's untitled live-action _[Bratz](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bratz "Bratz")_ film; she is in talks to play the film's antagonist, as of June 2025.[\[194\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-195)

## Public image

### Reception

Since rising to prominence in the late 2000s, Kim has remained a highly polarizing public figure. While critics have often dismissed her as being "famous for being famous", others have credited her with reshaping the nature of modern celebrity and the influence of [reality television](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reality_television "Reality television") and [social media](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Social_media "Social media") on fame.[\[195\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-196)

In 2010, [Barbara Walters](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Barbara_Walters "Barbara Walters") included her in her annual special of the "10 Most Fascinating People".[\[196\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-197) A 2011 [Nielsen](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nielsen_ratings "Nielsen ratings") poll ranked her among the most searched-for personalities on the [Internet](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Internet "Internet").[\[197\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-198) In 2015, _[Time](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Time_100 "Time 100")_ included her on its list of the 100 most influential people in the world,[\[198\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-199) while _[Forbes](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Forbes "Forbes")_ has featured her multiple times in its [Celebrity 100](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celebrity_100 "Celebrity 100") list, citing her earnings from television, endorsements, and businesses.[\[199\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-200) She ranked 17th, 13th, and 10th in _[FHM](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FHM "FHM")_'s [100 Sexiest Women](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/FHM's_100_Sexiest_Women_(UK) "FHM's 100 Sexiest Women (UK)") poll in 2008, 2015, and 2016, respectively.[\[200\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-201)[\[201\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-202)[\[202\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-203)

Despite this recognition, she has also faced criticism. A 2012 [British](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom") survey named her among the "most annoying celebrities",[\[203\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-204) while cultural commentators have accused her of promoting [materialism](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Materialism "Materialism") and unrealistic [beauty standards](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beauty_standards "Beauty standards").[\[204\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-205)

### Persona

[![](https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/05/Kim_Kardashian_LF.JPG)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Kim_Kardashian_LF.JPG) Kim Kardashian in 2008

Much of Kardashian's public persona has been linked to her image as a glamorous [socialite](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Socialite "Socialite"), [fashion icon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fashion_icon "Fashion icon"), and entrepreneur. She has often been described as embodying the archetype of the "celebutante", a celebrity known primarily for lifestyle, appearances, and media ubiquity rather than artistic output.[\[205\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-206)

Her image has been shaped around carefully curated aesthetics: [bodycon dresses](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bodycon_dress "Bodycon dress"), contour makeup, high-fashion collaborations, and viral photoshoots, such as her 2014 _[Paper](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paper_(magazine) "Paper (magazine)")_ magazine cover, which popularized the phrase "break the internet".[\[206\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-207)

Writers have noted that Kardashian has used her [reality show](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Keeping_Up_with_the_Kardashians "Keeping Up with the Kardashians") persona—at times perceived as vain or superficial—to build a multifaceted brand spanning [cosmetics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/KKW_Beauty "KKW Beauty"), [shapewear](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Skims "Skims"), [mobile apps](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian:_Hollywood "Kim Kardashian: Hollywood"), and fragrances.[\[207\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-208)

### Catchphrases

Though not as tied to slogans as other reality stars, Kardashian has popularized phrases such as "break the internet" and "Bible" (used colloquially to emphasize sincerity), which have been associated with her public persona.[\[208\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-209)

### Media presence

Kardashian has consistently been a fixture of global media since the 2007 debut of _[Keeping Up with the Kardashians](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Keeping_Up_with_the_Kardashians "Keeping Up with the Kardashians")_. [Tabloids](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tabloid_journalism "Tabloid journalism"), entertainment outlets, and online platforms have documented her relationships, fashion, and personal life, making her one of the most photographed women of the 21st century.[\[209\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-210)

By the mid-2010s, she was one of the most followed personalities on [Instagram](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Instagram "Instagram"), with over 350 million followers as of 2025.[\[210\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-211) Her online visibility has fueled the rise of [influencer culture](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Influencer_marketing "Influencer marketing"), with commentators crediting her for transforming how celebrities monetize fame.[\[211\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-212)

Throughout her career, Kardashian has appeared on the covers of numerous international magazines, including _[Vogue](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vogue_(magazine) "Vogue (magazine)")_,[\[212\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-213) _[Harper's Bazaar](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper's_Bazaar "Harper's Bazaar")_,[\[213\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-214) _[Elle](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elle_(magazine) "Elle (magazine)")_, _[GQ](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GQ "GQ")_,[\[214\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-215) _[Cosmopolitan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cosmopolitan_(magazine) "Cosmopolitan (magazine)")_, _[Adweek](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adweek "Adweek")_,[\[215\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-216) _[C Magazine](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cardinal_Courier_Media#C_Magazine "Cardinal Courier Media")_,[\[216\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-217) and _[Paper](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paper_(magazine) "Paper (magazine)")_[\[217\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-218) in the United States; _[Elle](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elle_(magazine) "Elle (magazine)")_, _[Glamour](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Glamour_(magazine) "Glamour (magazine)")_,[\[218\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-219) and _[ES Magazine](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Evening_Standard "Evening Standard")_ in the United Kingdom; _[Vogue](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vogue_Paris "Vogue Paris")_ in France,[\[219\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-220) Italy, Turkey, and India; _[Vanity Fair](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vanity_Fair_(magazine) "Vanity Fair (magazine)")_ in Spain; _[L'Officiel](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/L'Officiel "L'Officiel")_ in Germany; _Remix_ in New Zealand; and _[The New York Times Style Magazine](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times_Style_Magazine "The New York Times Style Magazine")_ in Singapore.[\[220\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-221)

## Personal life

### Relationships

In 2000, at 19 years old, Kardashian [eloped](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elopement_(marriage) "Elopement (marriage)") with music producer [Damon Thomas](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Underdogs_(production_team) "The Underdogs (production team)").[\[221\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-PeopleBio-222) Thomas filed for divorce in 2003. Kardashian later blamed their separation on physical and emotional abuse on his part[\[222\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-223) and said she was high on [ecstasy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MDMA "MDMA") during their wedding ceremony.[\[223\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-224) Before her divorce was finalized, Kardashian began dating singer Ray J.[\[221\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-PeopleBio-222)

Kardashian then dated [Reggie Bush](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reggie_Bush "Reggie Bush"). Their relationship began after [Matt Leinart](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Matt_Leinart "Matt Leinart") introduced them at the 2007 [ESPY Awards](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ESPY_Award "ESPY Award"). They split on July 27, 2009[\[224\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-225) and got back together on September 28, 2009.[\[225\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-226)
Kardashian also briefly dated [NFL](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NFL "NFL") player [Miles Austin](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Miles_Austin "Miles Austin") in 2010.[\[226\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-227)

In May 2011, Kardashian became engaged to [NBA](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NBA "NBA") player [Kris Humphries](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kris_Humphries "Kris Humphries"), then of the [New Jersey Nets](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Jersey_Nets "New Jersey Nets"), whom she had been dating since October 2010.[\[227\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-228) They were married in a wedding ceremony on August 20 in [Montecito, California](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Montecito,_California "Montecito, California").[\[228\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-229) Earlier that month, she had released her "wedding fragrance" called "Kim Kardashian Love" which coincided with her own wedding.[\[54\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Fragrances-55)[\[229\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-230) A two-part TV special showing the preparations and the wedding itself aired on _E!_ in early October 2011, amidst what _[The Washington Post](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Washington_Post "The Washington Post")_ called a "media blitz" related to the wedding.[\[230\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-231) After 72 days of marriage, she filed for divorce from Humphries on October 31, citing [irreconcilable differences](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irreconcilable_differences "Irreconcilable differences").[\[231\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-232) Several news outlets surmised that Kardashian's marriage to Humphries was merely a publicity stunt to promote the Kardashian family's brand and their subsequent television ventures.[\[232\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-233) A man professing to be her former publicist, Jonathan Jaxson, also claimed that her short-lived marriage was indeed staged and a ploy to generate money. Kardashian filed a suit against Jaxson, saying his claims were untrue, and later settled the case that included an apology from Jaxson.[\[233\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-234) A widely circulated petition asking to remove all Kardashian-related programming from the air followed the split.[\[234\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-235) The divorce was subject to widespread media attention.[\[235\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-britannica-236)

[![](https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/Kim_Kardashian_and_Kanye_West_at_the_Met_Gala_in_2019.png/500px-Kim_Kardashian_and_Kanye_West_at_the_Met_Gala_in_2019.png)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Kim_Kardashian_and_Kanye_West_at_the_Met_Gala_in_2019.png) Kardashian with then-husband [Kanye West](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kanye_West "Kanye West") at the [Met Gala](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Met_Gala "Met Gala") in 2019

Kardashian began dating rapper and longtime friend [Kanye West](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kanye_West "Kanye West") in April 2012, while still legally married to Humphries.[\[236\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-237) Her divorce was finalized on June 3, 2013,[\[237\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-238) Kardashian and West became engaged on October 21, Kardashian's 33rd birthday,[\[238\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-239) and married on May 24, 2014, at [Forte di Belvedere](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belvedere_(fort) "Belvedere (fort)") in [Florence, Italy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florence "Florence").[\[239\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-240) Her wedding dress was designed by [Riccardo Tisci](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Riccardo_Tisci "Riccardo Tisci") of [Givenchy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Givenchy "Givenchy")[\[240\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-241) with some guests' dresses designed by designer [Michael Costello](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Costello_(fashion_designer) "Michael Costello (fashion designer)").[\[241\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-242) The couple's high status and respective careers have resulted in their relationship becoming subject to heavy media coverage; _[The New York Times](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times "The New York Times")_ referred to their marriage as "a historic blizzard of celebrity".[\[1\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Caramanica2015-1) West said Kardashian was his [muse](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muse "Muse").[\[242\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-243)

In January 2021, [CNN](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CNN "CNN") reported that the couple were discussing divorce[\[243\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-244) and on February 19, 2021, Kardashian officially filed for divorce.[\[244\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-245) In April 2021, they both agreed before court that they would end their marriage due to "irreconcilable differences" and agreed to joint custody of their four children. They also agreed that neither of them need spousal support.[\[245\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-246) In February 2022, Kardashian filed a complaint to the [Los Angeles Superior Court](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Los_Angeles_Superior_Court "Los Angeles Superior Court"), asking for a quicker proceedings in the divorce from West, saying that West was trying to delay it and saying that "Mr. West, by his actions, has made it clear that he does not accept that the parties' marital relationship is over."[\[246\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-247) Kardashian was declared legally single on March 2, 2022.[\[247\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-248) She subsequently dropped "West" as her legal last name and ended their marriage.[\[248\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-249) A post-divorce settlement was reached on November 29, 2022.[\[249\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-250)

Kardashian was in a relationship with actor and comedian [Pete Davidson](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pete_Davidson "Pete Davidson") from November 2021 to August 2022.[\[250\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-251)[\[251\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-252)[\[252\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-253) From September 2023 to March 2024, Kardashian was reportedly in a relationship with NFL wide receiver [Odell Beckham Jr.](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Odell_Beckham_Jr. "Odell Beckham Jr.")[\[253\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-254)[\[254\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-255)[\[255\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-256)

[![](https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/KardashianSisters%40JillStuartShow_9_1110_by_BettinaCirone42_%2810%29.jpg/500px-KardashianSisters%40JillStuartShow_9_1110_by_BettinaCirone42_%2810%29.jpg)](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:KardashianSisters@JillStuartShow_9_1110_by_BettinaCirone42_(10).jpg) At the [Mercedes-Benz](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mercedes-Benz "Mercedes-Benz") Fashion Week 2010. Left to right: fellow cast member [Jonathan Cheban](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jonathan_Cheban "Jonathan Cheban"), Kim Kardashian, sister [Kourtney](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kourtney_Kardashian "Kourtney Kardashian"), and [Scott Disick](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scott_Disick "Scott Disick") (Kourtney's then partner)

Since 2026, she has reportedly been in a relationship with British seven-time [Formula One](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Formula_One "Formula One") World Champion [Lewis Hamilton](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lewis_Hamilton "Lewis Hamilton").[\[256\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-257)[\[257\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-258)[\[258\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-259)

### Religion

Kim Kardashian is a [Christian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christians "Christians") and has described herself as "really religious".[\[259\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Whittaker2018-260) She was educated in [Christian schools](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christian_school "Christian school") of both the [Presbyterian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Presbyterian "Presbyterian") and Roman Catholic traditions.[\[259\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-Whittaker2018-260) In October 2019, she was baptized in an [Armenian Apostolic](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenian_Apostolic_Church "Armenian Apostolic Church") ceremony at the baptistery in the [Etchmiadzin Cathedral](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Etchmiadzin_Cathedral "Etchmiadzin Cathedral") complex and given the Armenian name Heghine (Հեղինէ).[\[260\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-261)

In April 2015, Kardashian and West traveled to the [Armenian Quarter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenian_Quarter "Armenian Quarter") of the [Old City](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_City_(Jerusalem) "Old City (Jerusalem)") in [Jerusalem](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jerusalem "Jerusalem") to have their daughter baptized in the [Armenian Apostolic Church](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenian_Apostolic_Church "Armenian Apostolic Church"), one of the oldest denominations of [Oriental Orthodox Christianity](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oriental_Orthodox_Churches "Oriental Orthodox Churches"). The ceremony took place at the [Cathedral of St. James](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cathedral_of_St._James,_Jerusalem "Cathedral of St. James, Jerusalem").[\[261\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-262) [Khloé Kardashian](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khlo%C3%A9_Kardashian "Khloé Kardashian") was appointed as the godmother.[\[262\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-263) In October 2019, Kim baptized her three younger children at the baptistery in the [Etchmiadzin Cathedral](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Etchmiadzin_Cathedral "Etchmiadzin Cathedral") complex, Armenia's mother church.[\[263\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-264)[\[264\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-265)

### Health and pregnancies

Kardashian has four children with Kanye West: two daughters (born 2013 and 2018) and two sons (born 2015 and 2019).[\[265\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-266)[\[266\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kim_Kardashian#cite_note-267)

Kardashian has publicly discussed difficulties during her first two pregnancies. She experienced [pre-eclampsia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pre-eclampsia "Pre-eclampsia") during her first, which forced her to deliver at 34 weeks.
